ARIE vol.048, 1925-1926


APPENDIX A.


A. List of copper-plates examined during the year 1925-26.
1
Placement
Mr. M.S.Sarma of theTelugu Encyclopaediaoffice.
Year
Eastern Chā-ḷukya.
King
…
Date
Śaka 982,Uttarāyaṇa-saṁkrānti.
Language and Script
Sanskrit
Remarks
Records the gift of the village Avaraṅga inKōlavarttana-vishaya as a bhōga to the godJalēśvaradēva in the village. The date ofthe coronation of the king is given as Śaka960.
2
Placement
Śrī L.N.Deb, Jubraj of Tek-kali.
Year
Eastern Gaṅ-ga.
King
Mahārāja Indravarman
Date
Vijayarājya-samvatsara87, Jyēshṭha,10th day.
Language and Script
Sanskrit in archaic characters
Remarks
From a set of impressions received in the officefrom the Jubraj of Tekkali. Registers thegrant of some land in the village Haribhaṭa,situated in the Kṛōshṭukavarttani, free oftaxes, as dēvāgrahāra for worship andofferings and repairs in the temple ofRāmēśvara-Bhaṭṭāraka. The king bears thetitle Rajasiṁgha. The inscription was com-posed by Vinayachandra, son of Bhānu-chandra, and was engraved by Stapuṇōju.
3
Placement
Mr. Narayana Rao Deshpande,B.A., L.L.B., Pleader, Dhar-war, through Mr. N.Lak-shminarayana Rao of thisoffice.
Year
WesternChāḷukya.
King
Hiriya Hemmāḷirāya
Date
Śaka 100 [9],Ānanda(wrong),Chaitra, śu.11, Monday.
Language and Script
Kannaḍa in Nāgarī
Remarks
Seems to register a gift of land to the templeof Mūlasthāna Kalidēva at Vuṇḍāvar (?) byBommeya-Nāyaka, a minister of the king whocalls himself a great devotee of Bhūtanātha-dēva. Refers to the siege of the fortressTōragallu during a great battle in which theking was victorious.
4
Placement
From the same gentlemanthrough Mr. Lakshmi-narayana Rao.
Year
Yādava
King
Siṅghaṇa
Date
Śaka 1173,Plavaṅga(wrong),Jyēshṭha,paurṇimā,Thursday,lunar eclipse.
Language and Script
Sanskrit in Nāgarī
Remarks
Records the gift of shares in the villageNiherüra to a number of brahmans by Malli-Śrēshṭhi, the son-in-law of Bīchirāya, thegovernor under the Yādava king.
5
Placement
The Tahsildar of Bezwada
Year
Reḍḍi
King
Anavēma-Reḍḍi
Date
Śaka 1272,Bahudhānya,Māgha, ba.amāvāsyā,Sunday,solar eclipse.
Language and Script
Telugu
Remarks
The king bears a number of birudas. Recordsthe formation of a village called Vēmavaramto the east of Koṇḍapalli and its grant toDuggirāla Rāmaliṅgam and MūlasthānamSōmaliṅgam, who were experts in theintricacies of the Āgamas and Śaiva-śāstras.It also gives the names of the brahmanswho performed worship in the temple andto whom some shares in the villages wereallotted.
6
Placement
Mr. N.Seshagiri Rao, Settle-ment Revenue Inspector,Dharmavaram taluk, Ananta-pur, through Mr. A.Ranga-svami Sarasvati of this office.
Year
Vijayanagara
King
Pratāpa-Dēvarāya
Date
Śaka 1339,Hēma(vi)ḷam-bi, Māgha,chaturdaśī,Śivarātri.
Language and Script
Telugu
Remarks
Gift of the village Nāgireḍḍipalle, as sarva-mānya, to the brahman Dēvarasa, son ofBhāskaradēva, by the king.

From the Tahsildar, Dharma-varam taluk, Anantapur.

Vijayanagara
King

Date

Sanskrit & Telugu in Nāgarī.
Remarks
Plates missing in the beginning. Registersthe grant of Timmasamudram in Kanagāni-palli a village in the Gutti sub-division, toAppaḷāchārya, son of Tiruvēṅkaṭa Tātā-chārya and grandson of Penugoṇḍa Appayā-chārya. The grant was engraved byŚrīmallāchārya. The sign-manual of theking is engraved in Telugu as ‘Śrī-Virūpāksha.’

Placement
From Mr. GārachāvaḍiPullayya, Clerk, FundOffice, Dharmavaram.
Year
Do.
King
Prauḍhadēvarāya
Date
Śaka 1095,(wrong), Vija-[ya*], Māgha,ba. 12.
Language and Script
Telugu
Remarks
Purports to register the grant of the tenurecalled dēśāyi-karaṇikam to a certain Tiru-mala-Mallarasu, by Mahāmaṇḍalēśvara Bhu-jabala Śōmadēvarāya-Mahārāya, an agent ofthe king, and gives a list of fields granted tohim as remuneration in several villages.
14
Placement
From the same gentleman
Year
Vijayanagara
King
Prauḍhadēvarāya, ruling atVidyānagara-paṭṭaṇa.
Date
Śaka 1095,Śrīmukha,Āśvija, ba.12.
Language and Script
Kannaḍa & Telugu
Remarks
Purports to record a similar grant by the king,of the dēśāhi-karaṇika right over the vaḷitasof Tummala, Kanagānipalle, Pappūru andYāḍiki, to Mallarasu, son of Nāgarasu andgrandson of Vīrarasu of the Kauṇḍinya-gōtra. The grant is said to have been madefor the merit of Virūpākshēśvara in the pre-sence of Kriyāśaktisvāmi. The villages ofVēlpu-maḍugu in the Tummala-sīma andMālyavantam in the Pappūru-sīma were eachrenamed as Prauḍhadēvarāyapuram. Theofficer was given lands in several places asremuneration.
15
Placement
From a resident of Rāvula-cheruvu village, through theTahsildar of Dharmavaramtaluk.
Year
Do.
King
Vijaya-Bukkarāya
Date
Śaka 1109,Jaya Āśvija,śu. 10.
Language and Script
Telugu
Remarks
Purports to register the conferment of thereḍḍirikam right over Dharmavaram, inequal shares, on two families during theregime of Samprati Tipparājayya over Pen-namāgāṇi in Gutti-rājya. Also specifiesseveral individuals as the holders of the vari-ous offices in the village, and the extent ofthe lands allotted to them. Mentions aChikka-Oḍeya as having constructed theDharmavaram tank and as having broughtthe idol of Chennakēśavasvāmi from Āne-gondi and consecrated it in the village.
16
Placement
From the Reḍḍi of Nasana-kota, same taluk, throughMr. A.Rangaswami Saras-vati.

Do.
King
Vīrapratāpa Bukkarāyadēva-Mahārāya, ruling fromVidyānagara.

Language and Script
Telugu
Remarks
The copper-plate bears on its top a solid imageof two figures riding one behind the other ona single horse, the group being overshadowedby a serpent-hood. Purports to register theconferment of the gauḍirika right over thevillage Nasana in the Kanagānipalle-sīma,a sub-division of Pālēṭisthaḷa in Gutti-rājya,to Peda Chōḍama-Reḍḍi, and enumerates thelands granted to him.

Tirumalai-Nāyaka
Date
Achchuta(Akshaya ?),Vaikāśi 3.
Language and Script

Remarks
Purports to record the permission which theking granted, on the occasion of his visitto Bāvālippāḷaiyappaṭṭu, (when he waspleased with the reception accorded to himby the chief and four families from thenorth), to a certain Oṇḍippuli-Nāyaka, tofound a village in the latter's name and toserve as a pāḷaiyakāraṉ of six villages underhim. The surplus of revenue after deduct-ing 370 poṉ for himself as the pāḷaiyakāraṉand 70 poṉ as nāṭṭāmai-mānibam, was directedto be sent to the kachchēri at Madurāpuri.

C.--Stone inscriptions copied in 1926.


1
Placement
On the north wall of the Āṭkoṇḍīś-vara temple at Iraniyur, Tirup-pattur taluk, Ramnad district.
Year
Pāṇḍya
King
Vīra-Pāṇḍyadēva
Date
10+1st year, Āḍi
Language and Script
Tamil
Remarks
Registers the order of the chief Gāṅgēyaṉ granting (1/2) māof land free of taxes for the maintenance of the fresh-water tank called Aṟpudakkūttaṉ-ūraṇi at Iraṇiyūr.
2
Placement
On the same wall
Year
Do.
King
Māṟavarman alias TribhuvanachakravartinKulaśēkharadēva, ‘who took allcountries’.
Date
16th year, Mārgaḻi
Language and Script
Tamil
Remarks
Records a sale of land by the residents of Iraṇiyūr toDakshiṇāmūrtti-Śiva, one of the disciples of MudaliyārMalaimāṉ-Dēvar, residing in the maṭha adjoining thetemple of Tirunaṭṭamāḍīśvaram-uḍaiya-Nāyaṉār atMalaiyūr-paṭṭaṇam alias Īḻaṅkoṇḍapāṇḍi-paṭṭaṇam.
3
Placement
Do.
Year
…
King
…
Date
Śaka 1423, Raudri,Tai 2.
Language and Script
Tamil
Remarks
States that a certain Tiruvēṭpūr-uḍaiyār of Iḷaiyāttaṅguḍialias Kulaśēkharapuram constructed a fresh-water tankat Iraṇiyūr and that certain others set up an image of thegoddess in the temple of Bhadrakāḷi-Ammaṉ to the southof it. Also records a grant of land as dēvadāna to thegoddess for worship and the special privileges granted tothe donor by the residents of Iraṇiyūr.

472
Placement
On a stone built into the west wallof the bathing shed of the Āśrā-mattu-chiṟa (tank) at Talip-paramba, Chirakkal taluk,Malabar district.
Year
…
King
…
Date
Kollam 700, Maka-ram 3, Jupiter inMīnam, Kali day(expressed bychronogram dug-dham śuddhi hētu-kam) 1689598.
Language and Script
Sanskrit verse in Malayāḷam
Remarks
Records the completion of this tank on this day. Containsa reflection on the necessity for performing good deedsin this life.

474
Placement
On a slab set up in the court-yardof the Nārāyaṇkaṇṇūr temple,Ramantali, same taluk anddistrict.
Year
…
King
…
Date
Kali 4029, day (ex-pressed by chro-nogram panthāva-kēśavōyam)1451471.
Language and Script
Archaic Vaṭṭeḻuttu
Remarks
Records that Muṇḍaṉ Koṟṟaḍai of Maṉattuṇai purchasedfrom Nambiyār Vikkirama-Rāma a field called Ayiṉi inKaviyalppuram and gave it to the temple of god Nara-śiṅga-Viṇṇagar-Dēvar for maintaining a perpetual lampand for providing offerings. The trading corporationcalled maṇigrāmattār of Iḷaṅgōppaṭṭaṇam were in chargeof the endowment.
